                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Friday, May 16, 2014
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-fstDuL9tGx0/U3LglUs0lUI/AAAAAAAAJEM/fGAfyGPxCTY/s1600/IMG_4968+copy.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="8972400249228835267" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="6684045509454027950" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="6684045509454027950">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     Lucie in the Sky with Diamonds
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-6684045509454027950" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      Shortly after receiving piCture pOlish
                      <b>
                       Sky
                      </b>
                      in the mail last week, it dawned on me that I now owned polishes called
                      <b>
                       Sky
                      </b>
                      and
                      <b>
                       Lucie
                      </b>
                      (close enough, haha!) I couldn't resist the opportunity to use the names as inspiration for some diamond nail art! ;)
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-fstDuL9tGx0/U3LglUs0lUI/AAAAAAAAJEM/fGAfyGPxCTY/s1600/IMG_4968+copy.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="480" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-fstDuL9tGx0/U3LglUs0lUI/AAAAAAAAJEM/fGAfyGPxCTY/s1600/IMG_4968+copy.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      The bases on all blue nails is three thin coats of piCture pOlish
                      <b>
                       Sky
                      </b>
                      , my index finger is two coats of piCture pOlish
                      <b>
                       Black
                      </b>
                      . I freehanded diamonds on my two accent nails using acrylic paint and Essie
                      <b>
                       No Place Like Chrome
                      </b>
                      , and added a silver rhinestone to my index finger. My pinky is a glitter gradient with Shimmer Polish
                      <b>
                       Lucie
                      </b>
                      . All nails are topped with two coats of Seche Vite.
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-dB7rjIWW1Rc/U3Lgm5jN4mI/AAAAAAAAJEU/bs0xfawbAyY/s1600/IMG_4974+copy.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="480" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-dB7rjIWW1Rc/U3Lgm5jN4mI/AAAAAAAAJEU/bs0xfawbAyY/s1600/IMG_4974+copy.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      I was a little worried about freehanding the diamonds, but I think they turned out super cute; I also love the graphic contrast that the black nail provides! What do you think of this mani? :)
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-footer">
